```python
for image_idx, image in images_dict.items():
    
    img_h = image["height"]
    img_w = image["width"]
    file_name = image["file_name"]

    annotations = annotations_dict[image_idx]

    lines = []

    for ann in annotations:
        x_left, y_left, width, height = ann["bbox"]
        raw_class_id = ann["category_id"]

        if raw_class_id == 1:
            class_id = 0  # Make Q1 = Class 0
        elif raw_class_id == 0:
            class_id = 1  # Make Q2 = Class 1
        elif raw_class_id == 2:
            class_id = 2  # Make Q3 = Class 2 (This one was fine!)
        elif raw_class_id == 3:
            class_id = 3  # Make Q4 = Class 3 (This one was fine!)
        else:
            class_id = raw_class_id

        w_norm = width / img_w
        h_norm = height / img_h
        x_cen = (x_left + (width / 2)) / img_w
        y_cen = (y_left + (height / 2)) / img_h

        line = f"{class_id} {x_cen:.6f} {y_cen:.6f} {w_norm:.6f} {h_norm:.6f}"
        lines.append(line)

    txt_filename = file_name.replace('.png', '.txt').replace('.jpg', '.txt')
    out_filepath = Path(TRAIN_OUT) / txt_filename
        
    with open(out_filepath, 'w') as f:
        f.write('\n'.join(lines))
```


```python
TRAIN_IMAGES = Path("../data/stage 1/train/images")
TRAIN_LABELS = Path("../data/stage 1/train/labels")

VAL_IMAGES = Path("../data/stage 1/val/images")
VAL_LABELS = Path("../data/stage 1/val/labels")

VAL_IMAGES.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
VAL_LABELS.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

all_images = list(TRAIN_IMAGES.glob("*.png"))

n_to_val = 85

if len(all_images) < n_to_val:
    print(f"Error: Only found {len(all_images)} images. Can't move 50.")
else:
    images_to_move = random.sample(all_images, n_to_val)
    
    moved_count = 0
    
    for img_path in images_to_move:
        label_path = TRAIN_LABELS / f"{img_path.stem}.txt"
        
        if label_path.exists():
            new_img_dest = VAL_IMAGES / img_path.name
            new_label_dest = VAL_LABELS / label_path.name
            
            shutil.move(str(img_path), str(new_img_dest))
            shutil.move(str(label_path), str(new_label_dest))
            
            moved_count += 1
        else:
            print(f"Warning: No matching label found for {img_path.name}. Skipped.")
            
    print(f"Successfully moved {moved_count} image/label pairs to the validation folders!")
```

    Successfully moved 85 image/label pairs to the validation folders!



```python
def visualize_yolo_quadrants_random(images_dir: str, labels_dir: str):
    img_dir_path = Path(images_dir)
    lbl_dir_path = Path(labels_dir)
    
    quadrant_map = {
        0: {"name": "1 (Upper Right)", "color": "#00ff00"},
        1: {"name": "2 (Upper Left)",  "color": "#C56E17"},
        2: {"name": "3 (Lower Left)",  "color": "#5f92cd"},
        3: {"name": "4 (Lower Right)", "color": "#d633b8"}
    }

    all_images = list(img_dir_path.glob("*.png")) + list(img_dir_path.glob("*.jpg"))
    if not all_images:
        print(f"No images found in {img_dir_path}")
        return
        
    img_path = random.choice(all_images)
    label_path = lbl_dir_path / (img_path.stem + ".txt")

    img = Image.open(img_path)
    img_w, img_h = img.size

    fig, ax = plt.subplots(1, figsize=(16, 8))
    ax.imshow(img)
    ax.axis('off')
    ax.set_title(f"Quadrant Mapper Visualization | Image: {img_path.name}", fontsize=14)

    if label_path.exists():
        with open(label_path, 'r') as f:
            lines = f.readlines()
            
        for line in lines:
            parts = line.strip().split()
            if len(parts) != 5:
                continue
                
            class_id = int(parts[0])
            x_center = float(parts[1])
            y_center = float(parts[2])
            norm_w = float(parts[3])
            norm_h = float(parts[4])
            
            box_w = norm_w * img_w
            box_h = norm_h * img_h
            x_min = (x_center * img_w) - (box_w / 2)
            y_min = (y_center * img_h) - (box_h / 2)
            
            quad_info = quadrant_map.get(class_id, {"name": "Unknown", "color": "#ffffff"})
            quad_name = quad_info["name"]
            color = quad_info["color"]
            
            rect = patches.Rectangle(
                (x_min, y_min), box_w, box_h, 
                linewidth=3, edgecolor=color, facecolor='none'
            )
            ax.add_patch(rect)
            
            ax.text(
                x_min, y_min - 8, f"Quadrant {quad_name}", 
                color='black', fontsize=12, weight='bold',
                bbox=dict(facecolor=color, edgecolor='none', pad=3, alpha=0.8)
            )
    else:
        print(f"No label file found for {img_path.name}")

    plt.tight_layout()
    plt.show()
```


```python
visualize_yolo_quadrants_random(TRAIN_IMAGES, TRAIN_LABELS)
```

```python
images_dir = Path("../data/stage 1/val/images")
all_images = list(images_dir.glob("*.png"))

random_image = random.choice(all_images)
random_label = Path("../data/stage 1/val/" + random_image.name.split(".")[0] + ".txt")

random_image, random_label
```

```python
results = model.predict(
    source=str(random_image),
    device="mps", 
    conf=0.01,
    iou=0.999,
    max_det=5000
)

result = results[0]
predicted_boxes = result.boxes

len(predicted_boxes)
```

```python
def filter_bboxes(predicted_boxes):
    bboxes = []
    confs = []
    cls_ids = []

    for i in [0, 1, 2, 3]:
        class_indexes = torch.where(predicted_boxes.cls == i)[0]
        
        if len(class_indexes) > 0:
            best_idx = class_indexes[0].item()
            
            bboxes.append(predicted_boxes.xyxy[best_idx])
            confs.append(predicted_boxes.conf[best_idx])
            cls_ids.append(i)

    bboxes = torch.stack(bboxes)
    confs = torch.stack(confs).unsqueeze(1)
    cls_ids = torch.tensor(cls_ids, dtype=torch.float32).unsqueeze(1).to("mps")

    return torch.cat((bboxes, confs, cls_ids), dim=1) 
```


```python
new_data = filter_bboxes(predicted_boxes)
result.boxes = result.boxes.__class__(new_data, result.boxes.orig_shape)

res_plotted = result.plot()

plt.figure(figsize=(16, 8))
plt.imshow(cv2.cvtColor(res_plotted, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB))
plt.axis('off')
plt.title("Prediction", fontsize=16)
plt.show()
```

```python
def test_quadrant_model(model, num_images=10, custom_image_dir=None):
    if custom_image_dir:
        images_dir = Path(custom_image_dir)
    else:
        images_dir = Path("../data/stage 1/val/images") 
        
    all_images = list(images_dir.glob("*.png")) + list(images_dir.glob("*.jpg")) + list(images_dir.glob("*.jpeg"))
    
    if not all_images:
        print(f"No images found in {images_dir}")
        return
        
    if len(all_images) < num_images:
        num_images = len(all_images)
        
    test_images = random.sample(all_images, num_images)
    
    fig, axes = plt.subplots(nrows=num_images, ncols=1, figsize=(16, 8 * num_images))
    
    if num_images == 1:
        axes = [axes]

    for i, test_image in enumerate(test_images):
        results = model.predict(source=str(test_image), device='mps', conf=0.5, verbose=False) 
        result = results[0]
        predicted_boxes = result.boxes

        filtered_boxes = filter_bboxes(predicted_boxes)
        result.boxes = result.boxes.__class__(new_data, result.boxes.orig_shape)
        
        res_plotted = result.plot()
        img_h, img_w = res_plotted.shape[:2]
        
        label_path = Path(str(test_image).replace('/images/', '/labels/')).with_suffix('.txt')
        
        if label_path.exists():
            target_color = (0, 255, 0) 
            
            with open(label_path, 'r') as f:
                lines = f.readlines()
                
            for line in lines:
                parts = line.strip().split()
                if len(parts) == 5:
                    cls_id = int(parts[0])
                    x_cen = float(parts[1])
                    y_cen = float(parts[2])
                    w_norm = float(parts[3])
                    h_norm = float(parts[4])
                    
                    box_w = w_norm * img_w
                    box_h = h_norm * img_h
                    x_min = int((x_cen * img_w) - (box_w / 2))
                    y_min = int((y_cen * img_h) - (box_h / 2))
                    x_max = int(x_min + box_w)
                    y_max = int(y_min + box_h)
                    
                    cv2.rectangle(res_plotted, (x_min, y_min), (x_max, y_max), target_color, 3)
                    
                    target_name = result.names[cls_id]
                    cv2.putText(
                        res_plotted, f"TARGET: {target_name}", (x_min, y_min - 10),
                        cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.8, target_color, 2
                    )
        
        axes[i].imshow(cv2.cvtColor(res_plotted, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB))
        axes[i].axis('off')
        axes[i].set_title(f"Prediction {i+1} | File: {test_image.name}", fontsize=16)

    plt.tight_layout()
    plt.show()
```


```python
test_quadrant_model(model, num_images=10)
```
